                <component
                  refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_AMA_price_pos"
                  componentClassID="Microsoft.OLEDBSource"
                  contactInfo="OLE DB-Quelle;Microsoft Corporation; Microsoft SQL Server; (C) Microsoft Corporation; Alle Rechte vorbehalten; http://www.microsoft.com/sql/support;7"
                  description="OLE DB-Quelle"
                  name="Source_AMA_price_pos"
                  usesDispositions="true"
                  version="7">
                  <properties>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Die Anzahl der Sekunden für das Timeout eines Befehls. Der Wert &quot;0&quot; zeigt einen unendlichen Timeoutwert an."
                      name="CommandTimeout">0</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts an."
                      name="OpenRowset"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt die Variable an, die den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts enthält."
                      name="OpenRowsetVariable"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Der auszuführende SQL-Befehl."
                      name="SqlCommand"
                      UITypeEditor="Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls.ModalMultilineStringEditor, Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls, Version=14.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=89845dcd8080cc91">/*Maximales Datum im einem Monat*/
WITH	cteDatum	(products_id,Monat,Datum)
AS		(SELECT		sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6) AS Monat
					,MAX(sw_price_analysis_date)
		 FROM		sw_price_position
		 GROUP BY	sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)
)		

SELECT	SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)+'01' AS DateKey
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id AS Anbieter
		,MAX(p.products_id) AS Products_Id
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price AS Price
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position AS Pos_mit_Versandkosten
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs AS Versandkosten
		,(swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) AS Price_ohne_Versandkosten
		,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY swpp.sw_products_id, cteDatum.Datum ORDER BY (swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) ASC) AS Pos_ohne_Versandkosten
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_1
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=2 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_2
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_3
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=4 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_4
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=5 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_5
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=6 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_6
FROM	sw_price_position swpp
LEFT JOIN	sw_products sw ON sw.sw_products_id=swpp.sw_products_id
INNER JOIN	cteDatum ON cteDatum.products_id=swpp.sw_products_id AND cteDatum.Datum=swpp.sw_price_analysis_date
LEFT JOIN	[MigrationAmailo].[dbo].[products] p ON sw.sw_products_ean=p.products_ean
WHERE		sw.sw_products_ean&lt;&gt;' ' AND p.products_id IS NOT NULL AND sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=20
GROUP BY	swpp.sw_products_id
			,sw_price_analysis_date
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs
			,cteDatum.Datum</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Die Variable, die den auszuführenden SQL-Befehl enthält."
                      name="SqlCommandVariable"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Gibt die zu verwendende Spaltencodepage an, wenn keine Codepageinformationen von der Datenquelle verfügbar sind."

                  </properties>

                      name="OleDbConnection" />

                    <output
                      refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_AMA_price_pos.Outputs[Ausgabe der OLE DB-Quelle]"

                        <outputColumn

                <component
                  refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_CSW_price_pos"
                  componentClassID="Microsoft.OLEDBSource"
                  contactInfo="OLE DB-Quelle;Microsoft Corporation; Microsoft SQL Server; (C) Microsoft Corporation; Alle Rechte vorbehalten; http://www.microsoft.com/sql/support;7"
                  description="OLE DB-Quelle"
                  name="Source_CSW_price_pos"
                  usesDispositions="true"
                  version="7">
                  <properties>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Die Anzahl der Sekunden für das Timeout eines Befehls. Der Wert &quot;0&quot; zeigt einen unendlichen Timeoutwert an."
                      name="CommandTimeout">0</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts an."
                      name="OpenRowset"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt die Variable an, die den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts enthält."
                      name="OpenRowsetVariable"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Der auszuführende SQL-Befehl."
                      name="SqlCommand"
                      UITypeEditor="Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls.ModalMultilineStringEditor, Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls, Version=14.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=89845dcd8080cc91">/*Maximales Datum im einem Monat*/
WITH	cteDatum	(products_id,Monat,Datum)
AS		(SELECT		sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6) AS Monat
					,MAX(sw_price_analysis_date)
		 FROM		sw_price_position
		 GROUP BY	sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)
)		

SELECT	SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)+'01' AS DateKey
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id AS Anbieter
		,MAX(p.products_id) AS Products_Id
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price AS Price
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position AS Pos_mit_Versandkosten
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs AS Versandkosten
		,(swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) AS Price_ohne_Versandkosten
		,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY swpp.sw_products_id, cteDatum.Datum ORDER BY (swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) ASC) AS Pos_ohne_Versandkosten
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_1
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=2 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_2
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_3
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=4 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_4
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=5 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_5
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=6 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_6
FROM	sw_price_position swpp
LEFT JOIN	sw_products sw ON sw.sw_products_id=swpp.sw_products_id
INNER JOIN	cteDatum ON cteDatum.products_id=swpp.sw_products_id AND cteDatum.Datum=swpp.sw_price_analysis_date
LEFT JOIN	[MigrationCSW].[dbo].[products] p ON sw.sw_products_ean=p.products_ean
WHERE		sw.sw_products_ean&lt;&gt;' ' AND p.products_id IS NOT NULL AND sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=20
GROUP BY	swpp.sw_products_id
			,sw_price_analysis_date
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs
			,cteDatum.Datum</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Die Variable, die den auszuführenden SQL-Befehl enthält."
                      name="SqlCommandVariable"></property>

                <component
                  refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_ESW_price_pos"
                  componentClassID="Microsoft.OLEDBSource"
                  contactInfo="OLE DB-Quelle;Microsoft Corporation; Microsoft SQL Server; (C) Microsoft Corporation; Alle Rechte vorbehalten; http://www.microsoft.com/sql/support;7"
                  description="OLE DB-Quelle"
                  name="Source_ESW_price_pos"
                  usesDispositions="true"
                  version="7">
                  <properties>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Die Anzahl der Sekunden für das Timeout eines Befehls. Der Wert &quot;0&quot; zeigt einen unendlichen Timeoutwert an."
                      name="CommandTimeout">0</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts an."
                      name="OpenRowset"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt die Variable an, die den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts enthält."
                      name="OpenRowsetVariable"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Der auszuführende SQL-Befehl."
                      name="SqlCommand"
                      UITypeEditor="Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls.ModalMultilineStringEditor, Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls, Version=14.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=89845dcd8080cc91">/*Maximales Datum im einem Monat*/
WITH	cteDatum	(products_id,Monat,Datum)
AS		(SELECT		sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6) AS Monat
					,MAX(sw_price_analysis_date)
		 FROM		sw_price_position
		 GROUP BY	sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)
)		

SELECT	SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)+'01' AS DateKey
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id AS Anbieter
		,MAX(p.products_id) AS Products_Id
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price AS Price
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position AS Pos_mit_Versandkosten
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs AS Versandkosten
		,(swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) AS Price_ohne_Versandkosten
		,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY swpp.sw_products_id, cteDatum.Datum ORDER BY (swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) ASC) AS Pos_ohne_Versandkosten
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_1
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=2 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_2
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_3
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=4 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_4
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=5 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_5
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=6 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_6
FROM	sw_price_position swpp
LEFT JOIN	sw_products sw ON sw.sw_products_id=swpp.sw_products_id
INNER JOIN	cteDatum ON cteDatum.products_id=swpp.sw_products_id AND cteDatum.Datum=swpp.sw_price_analysis_date
LEFT JOIN	[MigrationESW].[dbo].[products] p ON sw.sw_products_ean=p.products_ean
WHERE		sw.sw_products_ean&lt;&gt;' ' AND p.products_id IS NOT NULL AND sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=20
GROUP BY	swpp.sw_products_id
			,sw_price_analysis_date
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs
			,cteDatum.Datum</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Die Variable, die den auszuführenden SQL-Befehl enthält."
                      name="SqlCommandVariable"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Gibt die zu verwendende Spaltencodepage an, wenn keine Codepageinformationen von der Datenquelle verfügbar sind."

                      name="AlwaysUseDefaultCodePage">false</property>

                      name="AccessMode"
                      typeConverter="AccessMode">2</property>
                    <property

                      description="Die Zuordnungen zwischen den Parametern im SQL-Befehl und den Variablen."

                <component
                  refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_HGO_price_pos"
                  componentClassID="Microsoft.OLEDBSource"
                  contactInfo="OLE DB-Quelle;Microsoft Corporation; Microsoft SQL Server; (C) Microsoft Corporation; Alle Rechte vorbehalten; http://www.microsoft.com/sql/support;7"
                  description="OLE DB-Quelle"
                  name="Source_HGO_price_pos"
                  usesDispositions="true"
                  version="7">
                  <properties>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Die Anzahl der Sekunden für das Timeout eines Befehls. Der Wert &quot;0&quot; zeigt einen unendlichen Timeoutwert an."
                      name="CommandTimeout">0</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts an."
                      name="OpenRowset"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt die Variable an, die den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts enthält."
                      name="OpenRowsetVariable"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Der auszuführende SQL-Befehl."
                      name="SqlCommand"
                      UITypeEditor="Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls.ModalMultilineStringEditor, Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls, Version=14.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=89845dcd8080cc91">/*Maximales Datum im einem Monat*/
WITH	cteDatum	(products_id,Monat,Datum)
AS		(SELECT		sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6) AS Monat
					,MAX(sw_price_analysis_date)
		 FROM		sw_price_position
		 GROUP BY	sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)
)		

SELECT	SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)+'01' AS DateKey
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id AS Anbieter
		,MAX(p.products_id) AS Products_Id
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price AS Price
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position AS Pos_mit_Versandkosten
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs AS Versandkosten
		,(swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) AS Price_ohne_Versandkosten
		,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY swpp.sw_products_id, cteDatum.Datum ORDER BY (swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) ASC) AS Pos_ohne_Versandkosten
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_1
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=2 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_2
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_3
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=4 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_4
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=5 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_5
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=6 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_6
FROM	sw_price_position swpp
LEFT JOIN	sw_products sw ON sw.sw_products_id=swpp.sw_products_id
INNER JOIN	cteDatum ON cteDatum.products_id=swpp.sw_products_id AND cteDatum.Datum=swpp.sw_price_analysis_date
LEFT JOIN	[MigrationHGO].[dbo].[products] p ON sw.sw_products_ean=p.products_ean
WHERE		sw.sw_products_ean&lt;&gt;' ' AND p.products_id IS NOT NULL AND sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=20
GROUP BY	swpp.sw_products_id
			,sw_price_analysis_date
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs
			,cteDatum.Datum</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Die Variable, die den auszuführenden SQL-Befehl enthält."
                      name="SqlCommandVariable"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Gibt die zu verwendende Spaltencodepage an, wenn keine Codepageinformationen von der Datenquelle verfügbar sind."
                      name="DefaultCodePage">1252</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Boolean"

                      name="AlwaysUseDefaultCodePage">false</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Gibt den zum Zugreifen auf die Datenbank verwendeten Modus an."
                      name="AccessMode"
                      typeConverter="AccessMode">2</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Die Zuordnungen zwischen den Parametern im SQL-Befehl und den Variablen."
                      name="ParameterMapping"></property>
                  </properties>

                    <output

                      <outputColumns>
                        <outputColumn
                          refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_HGO_price_pos.Outputs[Ausgabe der OLE DB-Quelle].Columns[Anbieter]"

                          errorRowDisposition="FailComponent"

                          truncationRowDisposition="FailComponent" />
                        <outputColumn
                          refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_HGO_price_pos.Outputs[Ausgabe der OLE DB-Quelle].Columns[Price]"

                          name="Price"
                          precision="15"

                          truncationRowDisposition="FailComponent" />
                        <outputColumn
                          refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_HGO_price_pos.Outputs[Ausgabe der OLE DB-Quelle].Columns[Versandkosten]"
                          dataType="numeric"

                <component
                  refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_SPO_price_pos"
                  componentClassID="Microsoft.OLEDBSource"
                  contactInfo="OLE DB-Quelle;Microsoft Corporation; Microsoft SQL Server; (C) Microsoft Corporation; Alle Rechte vorbehalten; http://www.microsoft.com/sql/support;7"
                  description="OLE DB-Quelle"
                  name="Source_SPO_price_pos"
                  usesDispositions="true"
                  version="7">
                  <properties>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Die Anzahl der Sekunden für das Timeout eines Befehls. Der Wert &quot;0&quot; zeigt einen unendlichen Timeoutwert an."
                      name="CommandTimeout">0</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts an."
                      name="OpenRowset"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Gibt die Variable an, die den Namen des zum Öffnen eines Rowsets verwendeten Datenbankobjekts enthält."
                      name="OpenRowsetVariable"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Der auszuführende SQL-Befehl."
                      name="SqlCommand"
                      UITypeEditor="Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls.ModalMultilineStringEditor, Microsoft.DataTransformationServices.Controls, Version=14.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=89845dcd8080cc91">/*Maximales Datum im einem Monat*/
WITH	cteDatum	(products_id,Monat,Datum)
AS		(SELECT		sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6) AS Monat
					,MAX(sw_price_analysis_date)
		 FROM		sw_price_position
		 GROUP BY	sw_products_id
					,SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)
)		

SELECT	SUBSTRING(CONVERT(CHAR(8),sw_price_analysis_date,112),1,6)+'01' AS DateKey
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id AS Anbieter
		,MAX(p.products_id) AS Products_Id
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price AS Price
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position AS Pos_mit_Versandkosten
		,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs AS Versandkosten
		,(swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) AS Price_ohne_Versandkosten
		,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY swpp.sw_products_id, cteDatum.Datum ORDER BY (swpp.sw_price_analysis_price-swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs) ASC) AS Pos_ohne_Versandkosten
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_1
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=2 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_2
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_3
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=4 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_4
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=5 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_5
		,CASE	WHEN	swpp.sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=6 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Top_6
FROM	sw_price_position swpp
LEFT JOIN	sw_products sw ON sw.sw_products_id=swpp.sw_products_id
INNER JOIN	cteDatum ON cteDatum.products_id=swpp.sw_products_id AND cteDatum.Datum=swpp.sw_price_analysis_date
LEFT JOIN	[MigrationSportona].[dbo].[products] p ON sw.sw_products_ean=p.products_ean
WHERE		sw.sw_products_ean&lt;&gt;' ' AND p.products_id IS NOT NULL AND sw_price_analysis_position&lt;=20
GROUP BY	swpp.sw_products_id
			,sw_price_analysis_date
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_stores_id
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_price
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_position
			,swpp.sw_price_analysis_shipping_costs
			,cteDatum.Datum</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Die Variable, die den auszuführenden SQL-Befehl enthält."
                      name="SqlCommandVariable"></property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Gibt die zu verwendende Spaltencodepage an, wenn keine Codepageinformationen von der Datenquelle verfügbar sind."
                      name="DefaultCodePage">1252</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Boolean"
                      description="Erzwingt die Verwendung des DefaultCodePage-Eigenschaftswerts beim Beschreiben von Zeichendaten."
                      name="AlwaysUseDefaultCodePage">false</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.Int32"
                      description="Gibt den zum Zugreifen auf die Datenbank verwendeten Modus an."
                      name="AccessMode"
                      typeConverter="AccessMode">2</property>
                    <property
                      dataType="System.String"
                      description="Die Zuordnungen zwischen den Parametern im SQL-Befehl und den Variablen."
                      name="ParameterMapping"></property>
                  </properties>
                  <connections>
                    <connection
                      refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_SPO_price_pos.Connections[OleDbConnection]"
                      connectionManagerID="Package.ConnectionManagers[core-sql2016.ShadowSportona]"
                      connectionManagerRefId="Package.ConnectionManagers[core-sql2016.ShadowSportona]"
                      description="Die für den Zugriff auf die Datenbank verwendete OLE DB-Laufzeitverbindung."
                      name="OleDbConnection" />
                  </connections>
                  <outputs>
                    <output
                      refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_SPO_price_pos.Outputs[Ausgabe der OLE DB-Quelle]"
                      name="Ausgabe der OLE DB-Quelle">
                      <outputColumns>
                        <outputColumn
                          refId="Package\Sequenzcontainer 1\DF_FactPricePosition\Source_SPO_price_pos.Outputs[Ausgabe der OLE DB-Quelle].Columns[Anbieter]"
                          dataType="i4"
